## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator. The acceleration dv_dt is determined by restoring forces (functions of x), damping forces (functions of v), possible external driving (functions of t), and nonlinear coupling terms between these variables.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Duffing with damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + linear damping)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (1 + c2 * x**2) (nonlinear damping)
- Driven oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * sin(c3 * t) (sinusoidal external forcing)
- Driven Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) + c2 * v (time-modulated stiffness)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity damping)
- Coulomb-like friction: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * (c2 + c3 * v**2) (combined linear and nonlinear damping)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 * v + c2 * v (quadratic position-dependent damping)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (amplitude-dependent frequency)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (Rayleigh-type nonlinear damping)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x³, x⁵) → preserve symmetry of oscillation about equilibrium
- Velocity-dependent terms (v, v³) → energy dissipation or self-excitation (damping/driving)
- Product terms x²v or v²x → amplitude-dependent damping, characteristic of limit cycle oscillators
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → external periodic driving force or parametric excitation
- Sign-preserving nonlinearity in restoring force (odd powers of x) → bounded oscillatory solutions
- Negative linear damping + positive cubic damping (c1*v + c2*v³ with opposite signs) → self-sustained oscillations / limit cycles
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous system, energy-based analysis applicable
- Even powers of x multiplying v (x²*v) → position-dependent damping coefficient, van der Pol type behavior
